# Groupings of all ligands that may be found in the BioLiP structural database
# The 4 nucleic acids entries ("NUCACID_") include: NUCDNA, NUCDNAB, NUCRNA, NUCRNAB
# The 2 DNA entries ("DNA_") include: NUCDNA, NUCDNAB
# The 2 RNA entries ("RNA_") include: NUCRNA, NUCRNAB
# All 204 ion entries ("ION_") were extracted from wwPDB's Chemical Component Dictionary (http://www.wwpdb.org/data/ccd),
# All 8428 drug entries ("DRUGLIKE_") were identified by comparing ligand SMILES strings (Tanimoto coefficient > 0.9) 
#  to drug SMILES strings obtained from DrugBank (https://www.drugbank.ca/releases/latest)
# All 4070 metabolite entries ("METABOLITE_") were identified by comparing ligand SMILES strings (Tanimoto coefficient > 0.9) 
#  to *endogenous metabolite* SMILES strings from the Human Metabolome Database
#  (http://www.hmdb.ca/system/downloads/current/hmdb_metabolites.zip)
# LAST UPDATED: September 26, 2018
